	focus = {#空军基地建设
		id = PRC_Air_base
		icon = GFX_focus_PRC_Air_base
		cost = 2.15

		completion_reward = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {

							not = {

						} 
					}

					}

					instant_build = yes

					type = anti_air_building
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes

			}

							not = {

			is_subject = no
			any_country = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					NOT = { 
						ROOT = {
							has_wargoal_against = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { 
					ROOT = {
						create_wargoal = {
							type = annex_everything
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							has_government = fascism
						}
						ROOT = { 
							remove_from_faction = PREV 
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = { 
						leave_faction = yes 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
